## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca7aa-1055">Attributs Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca7aa-1055">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ca7aa-1056">Cette classe contient les attributs suivants pour Windows Server 2008 :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca7aa-1056">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
